# Architectural Alignment: Unified Pipeline Model

> **Date:** 2026-05-13
> **Session ID:** `fab94abb`

---

## 1. Implementation Plan

# Architectural Alignment: Unified Pipeline Model

The user observed that `doc_parser` and `proofreader` diverge from `audio_transcriber`'s elegant `PipelineBase` execution flow. 
- `doc_parser` uses a custom `QueueManager` and `process_all()` which processes *all phases per file* rather than *all files per phase*. It also duplicates the CLI menu logic.
- `proofreader` manually implements the loop and menu in each phase and crashed due to a missing method (`get_status`) in the hand-rolled implementation.

To achieve 100% alignment, we will enforce the `audio_transcriber` model across all three skills.

## Core Directives
1. **Phase Execution**: All skills must be launched via `PipelineBase.run_skill_pipeline()`.
2. **Task Iteration**: All phase implementations must use `self.process_tasks(self._process_file)` to benefit from built-in state checking, checkpoints, health monitoring, and the interactive menu.
3. **State Syncing**: `StateManager` must accurately reflect the tasks.

## Refactoring `proofreader`

Since `proofreader` sources from two different places (`doc_parser` and `audio_transcriber`), its `StateManager` cannot just use a single `sync_physical_files()`.
We will modify `proofreader/scripts/run_all.py` to manually populate `StateManager` before running the pipeline:
1. Scan `doc_parser/output/01_processed` and `audio_transcriber/output/03_merged`.
2. Populate `state_manager.state` with all found documents and transcripts.
3. Call `self.process_tasks()` in `p01`, `p02`, and `p03` instead of the custom loops I built.

## Refactoring `doc_parser`

`doc_parser` is currently a monolithic Queue that runs all steps on a single PDF before moving to the next. The `audio_transcriber` model runs Phase 1 on all files, then Phase 2 on all files.
However, `doc_parser`'s DAG tracks `P0a`, `P1a`, `P1b`, `P1c`, `P1d`.
We will restructure `doc_parser/scripts/run_all.py` to:
1. Define formal Phase classes (e.g., `Phase0aDiagnostic`, `Phase0bImageExtraction`, `Phase1aTextExtraction`) that inherit from `PipelineBase`.
2. Inside each class's `run()` method, use `self.process_tasks()`.
3. `doc_parser/scripts/run_all.py` will then simply call `PipelineBase.run_skill_pipeline(phases=[...])`.

### Resolving the Conflict in `doc_parser`
`doc_parser` was designed as an asynchronous queue that fully processes one document end-to-end because parsing a PDF takes time and it was better to get a complete result out quickly. If we switch to horizontal phase execution (Phase 1 for all files -> Phase 2 for all files), it might delay the final output of the first PDF.

## User Review Required

**Important Question regarding `doc_parser`:**
`audio_transcriber` uses a "horizontal" pipeline: It transcribes *all* audio files first (Phase 1), then applies the glossary to *all* files (Phase 2), etc.
Currently, `doc_parser` uses a "vertical" queue: It takes one PDF and runs it entirely through all phases (Diagnosis, Extraction, VLM, OCR check) before starting the next PDF. 

If we strictly align `doc_parser` to the `audio_transcriber` architecture, it will become horizontal (it will extract text for all PDFs, and only when all are done will it start the VLM vision processing for all PDFs). 

Do you want `doc_parser` to become horizontal (like audio_transcriber), or should I adapt the `audio_transcriber` UI/Menu to wrap the vertical execution of `doc_parser` so it just *looks* the same without changing its execution order?


---

## 2. Walkthrough / Summary

# Doc Parser Pipeline Standardization Walkthrough

I have completed the migration of the OpenClaw `doc_parser` to the standardized `PipelineBase` architecture. This establishes a robust horizontal execution model identical to `audio_transcriber` and `proofreader`, bringing improved state management, granular dashboard reporting, and streamlined pipeline orchestration.

## 🛠️ Key Architectural Upgrades

### 1. `PipelineBase` Horizontal Phase Refactoring
All discrete phases in `doc_parser` have been refactored to inherit from `PipelineBase` and utilize `self.process_tasks()`:
- `Phase0aDiagnostic`
- `Phase0bPNGPipeline`
- `Phase1aPDFEngine`
- `Phase1bTextSanitizer`
- `Phase1bVectorChartExtractor`
- `Phase1cOCRQualityGate`
- `Phase1dVLMVision`

### 2. Standardized Orchestrator (`run_all.py`)
Replaced the legacy vertical `QueueManager` with a `DocParserOrchestrator` that:
- Coordinates execution using `PipelineBase.run_skill_pipeline()`.
- Implements extension-based state masking (`p0b` executes for PNGs; `p0a` to `p1d` execute for PDFs).
- Handles cross-phase dependencies natively using DAG checking in `StateManager`.

### 3. StateManager Expansion
- Upgraded `StateManager` to define `PHASES_PDF = ["p0b", "p0a", "p1a", "p1b_s", "p1b", "p1c", "p1d"]`.
- Modified `sync_physical_files()` to cleanly pick up `.pdf`, `.png`, `.jpg`, and `.jpeg` via multi-extension globbing.

### 4. Process Context and Fixes
- Unified `phase_key` attributes to align exactly with `StateManager` identifiers (e.g. `phase0a` → `p0a`, `phase1b_sanitizer` → `p1b_s`).
- Replaced custom state checks with the robust `_process_file(self, idx: int, task: dict, total: int)` signature across all phases.
- Restored `.publish()` mechanism to dispatch `DomainEvent("PipelineCompleted")` at the completion of `Phase 1d` and `Phase 0b`.

> [!NOTE]
> Testing via `uv run python skills/doc_parser/scripts/run_all.py` confirms that the pipeline dynamically differentiates PDFs and Image assignments, and appropriately ignores completed items based on the state matrix.

{"step_index":135,"source":"MODEL","type":"PLANNER_RESPONSE","status":"DONE","created_at":"2026-05-11T20:08:04Z","content":"`.gitignore` 檔案**不會直接影響專案在你「當前這台電腦」上的執行**，因為 Git 的忽略清單只決定哪些檔案不要被提交到版本庫（Version Control）。\n\n然而，它會**嚴重影響「在其他環境」的運行**（例如：將專案 clone 到新電腦、部署到伺服器，或交接給其他開發者時）。如果你的程式碼依賴了某些被 `.gitignore` 忽略的檔案或空目錄，專案在新環境就會啟動失敗或報錯。\n\n以下是這份 `.gitignore` 中，可能會影響專案在**新環境運行**的關鍵項目：\n\n### 1. 執行時目錄（Runtime Directories）\n- `openclaw-sandbox/data/`\n- `openclaw-sandbox/logs/`\n- `logs/`\n**風險與影響**：Git 不會追蹤這些目錄。如果你的 Python 程式碼或 Shell 腳本假設這些目錄已經存在，且在寫入檔案前沒有先執行 `os.makedirs(..., exist_ok=True)` 或 `mkdir -p`，專案就會因為 `FileNotFoundError` 而崩潰。\n\n### 2. 環境變數與金鑰（Secrets & Environment）\n<truncated 2022 bytes>"}

{"step_index":2153,"source":"MODEL","type":"PLANNER_RESPONSE","status":"DONE","created_at":"2026-05-13T03:00:48Z","content":"這兩個問題非常經典！我已經為您修復完畢，以下是導致這兩個問題發生的原因以及我的修復方式：\n\n### 1. Phase 2 (Transcript Proofread) 卡住不動（Deadlock）\n- **原因：** 您遇到的是典型的多執行緒「死鎖 (Deadlock)」。在 `p02_transcript_proofread.py` 中，為了載入參考資料呼叫了 `GlobalRegistry.get_asset_paths`，而這個方法取得 `_lock` 後，又在內部呼叫了同類別的 `get_assets`，後者又試圖取得同一個 `_lock`。因為原本使用的是 `threading.Lock()`（不可重入），所以造成了程式永遠卡在那裡等待自己釋放鎖。\n- **修復：** 我已將 `core/state/global_registry.py` 中的 `_lock = threading.Lock()` 改為支援重入的 `threading.RLock()`，徹底解決了卡死問題。\n\n### 2. The archival log may miss the final conversation turns if run before pushing.\n\n**原因**：`archive_session.py` 會把完整的對話記錄（包括 commit hash、最後幾輪的討論）一起封存進 `memory/sessions/`。如果在 push 之前封存，封存檔裡的 commit hash 會是舊的，且最後幾輪對話（包括封存確認本身）就會遺漏。所以正確順序是：**commit → push → archive**，現有 prompt 沒問題。\n\n---\n\n## 2. 加強版 Prompt\n\n以下是優化後的版本，核心改進是加入**動態 MD 掃描階段**：\n\n'''\n請執行對話結束流程：\n\n【Step 1 — Continuous Principle Sync】\n掃描本次對話，提取所有新原則或操作習慣。\n<truncated 3080 bytes>"}
